let jsonObjects = JSON.parse(events);
let forms = "";


let lastEventTime = now.getTime()-300000;

let putRequestOptions = {
		  method: 'PUT',
		  headers: {
			  "Authorization": "Bearer "+token ,
			  "Content-Type": "application/json"
		  },
		  body: "",
		  redirect: 'follow'
	};



 for(let counter = 0 ; counter < jsonObjects.length ; counter++){
 	
		if(counter+1==jsonObjects.length){
			jsonObjects[counter].eventTime.timestamp=lastEventTime;
		}
		else{
			let difference = jsonObjects[jsonObjects.length-1].eventTime.timestamp-jsonObjects[counter].eventTime.timestamp;
			jsonObjects[counter].eventTime.timestamp=lastEventTime-difference;
		}
 		let estDate = new Date(new Date(jsonObjects[counter].eventTime.timestamp).toLocaleString("en-US", {timeZone: "America/New_York"}));
		jsonObjects[counter].eventTime.logDate.date=getFormattedDate(estDate);	 
 		
		let raw = jsonObjects[counter];
		let jsonFormattedRaw = JSON.stringify(raw);
		putRequestOptions.body=jsonFormattedRaw;
		let eventId =raw._id;
		let url = "https://backend.apexhos.com/hos_events/"+eventId+"?%24client%5BignoreRev%5D=true&%24client%5BcreateIfNotExist%5D=false&%24client%5BuseServerAuditTime%5D=true";
		fetch(url, putRequestOptions)
		  .then(response => response.json());
		
		
 }
 
 console.log("done");
 
 
 
 function getFormattedDate(date){	
		const year = date.getFullYear();
		const month = padTo2Digits(date.getMonth() + 1);
		const day = padTo2Digits(date.getDate());
		const dateWithSlashes = [year, month, day].join('/');		
		return dateWithSlashes;	
}
 
 
 function padTo2Digits(num){
	return num.toString().padStart(2, '0');
}
